Tool calls:  [ToolUseBlock(id='toolu_01X1XGTt2tdV7uJaiyEyCf7C', input={'coworker_name': 'Sarah', 'message': "Sarah, here's a comprehensive approach to your market regime change prediction challenge:\n\nComprehensive Machine Learning Strategy for Market Regime Prediction\n\n1. Feature Engineering and Selection\n```python\nimport numpy as np\nimport pandas as pd\nfrom sklearn.feature_selection import mutual_info_classif, SelectKBest\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\n\nclass MarketRegimeFeatureProcessor:\n    def __init__(self, raw_features):\n        self.features = raw_features\n    \n    def engineer_features(self):\n        # Advanced feature engineering\n        def create_interaction_features(df):\n            # Cross-feature interactions\n            df['market_momentum'] = df['price_change'] * df['volume']\n            df['volatility_trend'] = df['volatility'].rolling(window=5).std()\n            df['sentiment_momentum'] = df['sentiment_score'] * df['news_volume']\n            return df\n        \n        # Technical indicator generation\n        def generate_technical_indicators(df):\n            df['RSI'] = self.calculate_rsi(df['close_price'])\n            df['MACD'] = self.calculate_macd(df['close_price'])\n            return df\n        \n        # Feature selection using mutual information\n        def select_top_features(X, y, k=15):\n            selector = SelectKBest(score_func=mutual_info_classif, k=k)\n            X_new = selector.fit_transform(X, y)\n            selected_features = selector.get_support(indices=True)\n            return X_new, selected_features\n\n    def calculate_rsi(self, prices, periods=14):\n        # Relative Strength Index calculation\n        delta = prices.diff()\n        gain = (delta.where(delta > 0, 0)).rolling(window=periods).mean()\n        loss = (-delta.where(delta < 0, 0)).rolling(window=periods).mean()\n        rs = gain / loss\n        return 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n\n    def calculate_macd(self, prices):\n        # MACD calculation\n        exp1 = prices.ewm(span=12, adjust=False).mean()\n        exp2 = prices.ewm(span=26, adjust=False).mean()\n        macd = exp1 - exp2\n        signal = macd.ewm(span=9, adjust=False).mean()\n        return macd - signal\n\n2. Model Architecture and Selection\n```python\nimport tensorflow as tf\nfrom sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import cross_val_score\n\nclass RegimeChangeModelEnsemble:\n    def __init__(self, features, labels):\n        self.features = features\n        self.labels = labels\n    \n    def build_neural_network(self):\n        model = tf.keras.Sequential([\n            tf.keras.layers.Dense(64, activation='relu', input_shape=(self.features.shape[1],)),\n            tf.keras.layers.Dropout(0.3),\n            tf.keras.layers.Dense(32, activation='relu'),\n            tf.keras.layers.Dropout(0.2),\n            tf.keras.layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')\n        ])\n        model.compile(optimizer='adam', \n                      loss='binary_crossentropy', \n                      metrics=['accuracy'])\n        return model\n    \n    def ensemble_prediction(self):\n        # Ensemble of multiple models\n        models = {\n            'logistic_regression': LogisticRegression(),\n            'random_forest': RandomForestClassifier(n_estimators=100),\n            'neural_network': self.build_neural_network()\n        }\n        \n        # Cross-validation and model comparison\n        model_performance = {}\n        for name, model in models.items():\n            if name == 'neural_network':\n                # Specific handling for neural network\n                scores = cross_val_score(model, self.features, self.labels, cv=5)\n            else:\n                scores = cross_val_score(model, self.features, self.labels, cv=5)\n            model_performance[name] = scores.mean()\n        \n        return model_performance\n\n3. Handling Rare Regime Changes\n```python\nfrom imblearn.over_sampling import SMOTE\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import StratifiedKFold\n\nclass ImbalancedDataHandler:\n    def __init__(self, X, y):\n        self.X = X\n        self.y = y\n    \n    def handle_class_imbalance(self):\n        # SMOTE for synthetic minority class generation\n        smote = SMOTE(random_state=42)\n        X_resampled, y_resampled = smote.fit_resample(self.X, self.y)\n        \n        return X_resampled, y_resampled\n    \n    def stratified_cross_validation(self):\n        # Stratified sampling to maintain class distribution\n        skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=5, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n        return skf.split(self.X, self.y)\n\n4. Evaluation Metrics\n```python\nfrom sklearn.metrics import (\n    precision_recall_curve,\n    average_precision_score,\n    roc_auc_score,\n    confusion_matrix\n)\n\ndef advanced_model_evaluation(y_true, y_pred, y_pred_proba):\n    # Comprehensive evaluation metrics\n    metrics = {\n        'precision_recall_curve': precision_recall_curve(y_true, y_pred_proba),\n        'average_precision': average_precision_score(y_true, y_pred_proba),\n        'roc_auc': roc_auc_score(y_true, y_pred_proba),\n        'confusion_matrix': confusion_matrix(y_true, y_pred)\n    }\n    \n    # Custom cost function for regime change prediction\n    def regime_change_cost_function(y_true, y_pred):\n        # Penalize missed regime changes more heavily\n        false_negative_cost = 5  # Higher cost for missing regime changes\n        false_positive_cost = 1\n        \n        cm = confusion_matrix(y_true, y_pred)\n        cost = (cm[0][1] * false_positive_cost + \n                cm[1][0] * false_negative_cost)\n        return cost\n\n    return metrics\n```\n\nRecommended Approach:\n1.
